  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }

      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',

        state: 'apple_oauth_state_78d0e421-35e2-4077-9452-4ebe31966e61'

<div id="review_525555094" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/525555094" />
    <a title="Gonca Yalcin" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/8609022-gonca-yalcin"><img alt="Gonca Yalcin" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1585319278p2/8609022.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/525555094?book_show_action=true">Feb 03, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Gonca Yalcin" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Gonca Yalcin" href="/user/show/8609022-gonca-yalcin">Gonca Yalcin</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer525555094" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7831217207450730530">The Vision was the best book in the series so far. I mean right now, after finishing the book, my emotions are all over the place. Gemma/Alex in this book was perfect. We see their true feelings for each other and how their relationship changes in this book. And most of the time I was fangirling hard over these two. Would it be too weird if I told you I actually <i>felt</i> the electricity between them? And also, Gemma becomes more confident in this book. And I loved it. I mean, she actually grows up i</span>
  <span id="freeText7831217207450730530" style="display:none">The Vision was the best book in the series so far. I mean right now, after finishing the book, my emotions are all over the place. Gemma/Alex in this book was perfect. We see their true feelings for each other and how their relationship changes in this book. And most of the time I was fangirling hard over these two. Would it be too weird if I told you I actually <i>felt</i> the electricity between them? And also, Gemma becomes more confident in this book. And I loved it. I mean, she actually grows up in this book. She makes her own decisions and tries to be the person she was meant to be. And this is really hard for Alex. Because he always wants to protect her, but he learns that he can't. Sometimes he has to let her go, and in this book, he does. And their relationship comes to a whole different level. Oh god, how I loved it. Anddd.. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[in the end, when he left to go find a way to save Gemma= MY HEART BROKE TO SO MANY PIECES, I SWEAR I FELT ME HEART BEING CRUSHED.ITS JUST UNBELIEVEABLE. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> . Another thing that I loved, really really loved in this book was how we saw the true Aislin. She has this dark side, the witch side of her which her father taught her well to hide under all those pink dresses. And Gemma realizes maybe they aren't really so different. I felt really bad for Aislin, I mean, she was taught to hide who she really is, and it must be really hard, I mean being a witch is in her blood right? And another thing I love is that in this book the <i>thing</i> between Laylen and Aislin is a little bit clarified in this book. Which I love. Oh, and I love Laylen! He is so broken, it breaks my heart. I am really happy for him, because now he is really really good friends with Gemma and things are getting better with Aislin and spoiler: <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[the last scene where him and Alex kind of bonded when Alex told Laylen he was going to leave, he cried for god's sake! <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> I loved this book, it was by far my favorite, and I'm really hoping there will be a happy ending in the last book, aka The Promise!</span>
  <a data-text-id="7831217207450730530" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer158088613564963429">So. Either this book is way shorter than the first two, or i read super fast. I really enjoyed this book (as well as the first two) but this one just felt more rushed. And - im not sure if this is the same with the actual book - but there were a lot of random question marks at the end of sentences...<br/><br/>So that annoyed me.<br/><br/>But, something else that annoyed me was the fact that there seems to be nothing with Laylen and Gemma. What is up with that?? I thought after the whole biting thing there would be </span>
  <span id="freeText158088613564963429" style="display:none">So. Either this book is way shorter than the first two, or i read super fast. I really enjoyed this book (as well as the first two) but this one just felt more rushed. And - im not sure if this is the same with the actual book - but there were a lot of random question marks at the end of sentences...<br /><br />So that annoyed me.<br /><br />But, something else that annoyed me was the fact that there seems to be nothing with Laylen and Gemma. What is up with that?? I thought after the whole biting thing there would be something... But no.<br /><br />I was also so sad when Nicholas died. He`s annoying and everything, but its funny, and i don't think he should have died. And then at the end it gets all complicated by him not really being dead...?<br /><br />At the end of the second book, i was like omg she is stuck in a cabin thing on her own and will like die, this is so interesting!!<br />But it only lasted for a chapter. And i still don't understand how she got out of there...<br /><br />I also noticed a lot of "one two three" moments in the book, but that may just be me being weird.<br /><br />However, no matter how weird, random, unfair and rushed it is;<br />It was still a great book to me.</span>

<div id="review_514301041" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/514301041" />
    <a title="Heather B (Owlnestly Reviews)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11679252-heather-b-owlnestly-reviews"><img alt="Heather B (Owlnestly Reviews)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1352734750p2/11679252.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/514301041?book_show_action=true">Jan 22, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Heather B (Owlnestly Reviews)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Heather B (Owlnestly Reviews)" href="/user/show/11679252-heather-b-owlnestly-reviews">Heather B (Owlnestly Reviews)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer514301041" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9126920020034147881">Owlnestly Reviews<br/><a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='http://owlnestlyreviews.blogspot.com'>http://owlnestlyreviews.blogspot.com</a><br/><br/>I don't normally review series as a whole, or the whole series, but this one I just had to. This author is a genius, literally a genius. One word to sum up my thoughts for this series is: OBSESSED. I read all four of these books in four days, they were that good. <br/><br/>At first I thought the series was going to be a bit cheesy, with the end of the world bit and all, but instead I ending up loving it. There were so many new concepts put into play lik</span>
  <span id="freeText9126920020034147881" style="display:none">Owlnestly Reviews<br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://owlnestlyreviews.blogspot.com">http://owlnestlyreviews.blogspot.com</a><br><br>I don't normally review series as a whole, or the whole series, but this one I just had to. This author is a genius, literally a genius. One word to sum up my thoughts for this series is: OBSESSED. I read all four of these books in four days, they were that good. <br><br>At first I thought the series was going to be a bit cheesy, with the end of the world bit and all, but instead I ending up loving it. There were so many new concepts put into play like tattoos for different beings (foreseers, keepers, vampires, witches, immortals, etc.) I found myself overwhelmed at first, but Sorensen explained everything so perfectly that I fell into the world of Gemma. <br><br>Gemma is one of those characters that grow on you. I found her a tad starnge at first because she said that she lived without emotions for her whole life. I wanted to just say "Hold up, how is that even possible?" but I found myself becoming very attached to Gemma and her fate. I did find myself becoming frustrated at her when she just kind of swooned over the jerk that was mean to her in the beginning, but throughout the series she became the kind of heroine that I love to see succeed. I wish that I had as much spunk and bravery that she does by the end of the series. Alex is another character that I found myself loving, despite his jerk able characteristics. I hated when he was a jerk to Gemma, but I understood everything and his actions as the story panned out. Laylen was another character that I wish I knew in real life. He was just a lost soul, but he was such a sweetheart. <br><br>The story itself is full of twists and turns that will leave you begging for me. I never got bored reading, and that is saying something since I do have a hint of ADD. I blazed through these books, as I am sure you will when you check this series out. I am so overwhelmed with obsession with these books and this author that I even have to use a gif, which I NEVER do. So here you go:<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380374055ra/727960.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="9126920020034147881" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer449571738" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11148212092587407624">I don't have a lot to say about this book because it's a filler book until the end of the series. This is about the time when I get frustrated that not enough people realize that a good book doesn't have to be split up into multiple sequential novels just because that's what you had planned. It's sort of the same feeling I have about movies that are from one book being split up into multiple sequential films. Just share the important information and forget about all the superfluous detail and gi</span>
  <span id="freeText11148212092587407624" style="display:none">I don't have a lot to say about this book because it's a filler book until the end of the series. This is about the time when I get frustrated that not enough people realize that a good book doesn't have to be split up into multiple sequential novels just because that's what you had planned. It's sort of the same feeling I have about movies that are from one book being split up into multiple sequential films. Just share the important information and forget about all the superfluous detail and give me more plot instead of biding your time! Anyway, I didn't enjoy this book as much as the rest in this series because of the filler effect, as I will now call it. Don't get me wrong, some interesting things did happen, but it seems like it was thrown in just to make this into a tetrology instead of a trilogy. Off to read the next one though!</span>

<div id="review_225356617" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

<div id="review_322951945" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/322951945" />
    <a title="Michelle&#39;s Paranormal Vault of Books" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/8875051-michelle-s-paranormal-vault-of-books"><img alt="Michelle&#39;s Paranormal Vault of Books" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1373846671p2/8875051.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/322951945?book_show_action=true">May 02, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Michelle&#39;s Paranormal Vault of Books" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Michelle&#39;s Paranormal Vault of Books" href="/user/show/8875051-michelle-s-paranormal-vault-of-books">Michelle&#39;s Paranormal Vault of Books</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8875051-michelle-s-paranormal-vault-of-books?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8875051-michelle-s-paranormal-vault-of-books?shelf=owned-e-books">owned-e-books</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer322951945" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4995564053433158609"><b>WOW!</b> Is one word to sum up this amazing 3rd installment to the Fallen Star Series. I, in a way was very lucky to have discovered this series late, meaning I started the first one, only a month or so, before the 4th was due out. SO when I got hooked, I was able to download the rest, and keep reading. This one was also "on the edge of your seat" amazing.<br/><br/><a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/4601855.Jessica_Sorensen' title='Jessica Sorensen' rel='nofollow noopener'>Jessica Sorensen</a> has really made Gemma a dynamic character as, looking back, I can see how she has morphed and changed into the strong willed youn</span>
  <span id="freeText4995564053433158609" style="display:none"><b>WOW!</b> Is one word to sum up this amazing 3rd installment to the Fallen Star Series. I, in a way was very lucky to have discovered this series late, meaning I started the first one, only a month or so, before the 4th was due out. SO when I got hooked, I was able to download the rest, and keep reading. This one was also "on the edge of your seat" amazing.<br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/4601855.Jessica_Sorensen" title="Jessica Sorensen" rel="nofollow noopener">Jessica Sorensen</a> has really made Gemma a dynamic character as, looking back, I can see how she has morphed and changed into the strong willed young woman that every heroine should be.<br><br>Even though I was familiar with the storyline, I wasn't actually prepared for the emotions that hit me during this book. <b>The Vision</b> was probably the most emotional book out of the series (so far) because we see Gemma's and Alex's relationship on a whole new level. Even though they are trying to find a way to be together they are thrown a whole new line of obstacles that honestly leave you emotionally drained in a good way. I, yet again, could not put the book down (well, my kindle) I am truly am amazed at Jessica's writing style. I read lots of books, and can honestly say she is one of my favorite writers now.<br><br>I highly recommend this book, and the whole series. Its AMAZING! Be sure to read <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/11051889.The_Fallen_Star__Fallen_Star___1_" title="The Fallen Star (Fallen Star, #1) by Jessica Sorensen" rel="nofollow noopener">The Fallen Star</a> and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/11714997.The_Underworld__Fallen_Star___2_" title="The Underworld (Fallen Star, #2) by Jessica Sorensen" rel="nofollow noopener">The Underworld</a> before this one. Then the 4th one after this one <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/12989115.The_Promise__Fallen_Star___4_" title="The Promise (Fallen Star, #4) by Jessica Sorensen" rel="nofollow noopener">The Promise</a><br><br>Make sure to check out my blog for more reviews and extras, will have author interviews there too. <br><a href="http://concisebookreviewsbymichelle.blogspot.com/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer414911914" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12152928866763608983">Gemma is given a second chance. She was held captive by Stephan and left to suffer alone. She finds her dad in the Room of Forbidden. He helps her change the past and future to save the world. She’s been given this Mapping Ball, which is the key to save the future. Alex and Gemma’s feelings grow more intense but they need to stay away from each other or else the star will fade and they will kill each other. Nicholas and Gemma make a blood promise to tell the truth, since he has been branded with</span>
  <span id="freeText12152928866763608983" style="display:none">Gemma is given a second chance. She was held captive by Stephan and left to suffer alone. She finds her dad in the Room of Forbidden. He helps her change the past and future to save the world. She’s been given this Mapping Ball, which is the key to save the future. Alex and Gemma’s feelings grow more intense but they need to stay away from each other or else the star will fade and they will kill each other. Nicholas and Gemma make a blood promise to tell the truth, since he has been branded with the Mark of Malefiscus. Nicholas dies in a car accident and due to a Death Walker. They find out where Laylen has been hiding. He met Stasha and went over to her place. Stasha is Alex’s ex-girlfriend. She has the power to kill people with her touch and she tries to kill Gemma out of jealousy. Gemma’s mom runs off to the Keeper’s Castle to kill Stephan. Laylen and Gemma set off to rescue her. Along the way, they find Aleesa. She’s a half-faerie/Keeper and Stephan’s daughter. He kept her secluded from the world. They save her and Gemma’s mom. Gemma finds out she’s a Keeper too during a fight with the Death Walkers. Everyone has been branded with the Mark of Malefiscus from Stephan. He’s working extra hard to try and capture Gemma. Aislin is working on a spell to remove that mark on Gemma’s mom. Gemma and Alex find the Keepers History book to find some answers. Gemma is looking for the Purple Flame with some help she finds it, goes into the Mapping Ball, which holds the truth about the future her father changed. Originally the world was going to end in fire and in ice once her father changed things. Gemma learns that to save the world, her and Alex have to sacrifice themselves. She changes things back to normal. Everyone is devastated about the news. Gemma’s mom tells her there’s always loopholes and to find hers. Gemma and Alex talk about the future and find out they want to spend it together. The end of the world has started… with fire. Alex leaves Gemma to save her and their future.</span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Carrie (Bears Read Too)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Carrie (Bears Read Too)" href="/user/show/5824840-carrie-bears-read-too">Carrie (Bears Read Too)</a>

          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781466415157" href="/book/show/12958028-the-vision">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5824840-carrie-bears-read-too?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer219896015" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4936824581014219102">I was hooked on this series from the very first paragraph of the first book. It took me a few chapters to finally delve into the meat and potatoes of the story but from the very first paragraph I knew I had to find out everything about this girl with the violet eyes. Her story intrigued me and called out to me with each word.<br/><br/>Well… pleasantly… the story went wayyy beyond the violet-eyed beauty. We learned of other AMAZING characters as well.<br/><br/>The green-eyed, gorgeous, dark-haired, scrumptious, masc</span>
  <span id="freeText4936824581014219102" style="display:none">I was hooked on this series from the very first paragraph of the first book. It took me a few chapters to finally delve into the meat and potatoes of the story but from the very first paragraph I knew I had to find out everything about this girl with the violet eyes. Her story intrigued me and called out to me with each word.<br /><br />Well… pleasantly… the story went wayyy beyond the violet-eyed beauty. We learned of other AMAZING characters as well.<br /><br />The green-eyed, gorgeous, dark-haired, scrumptious, masculine hero… and my personal favourite… Alex! He’s got quite a story himself that is dying to be told.<br /><br />His spunky bright-eyed witchy sister, Aislin and the somewhat laid back blonde-with-blue-tips hunky vampire, Laylen. <br /><br />I even have a small soft spot for Nicholas. It may be small, but it’s still there. <i>wink wink</i><br /><br />These four and their adventures together make up one of the best series that I’ve not only read this year, but read! Period! The friendship and loyalty that exude out of these people is so enjoyable to read. The refreshing idea of the story itself as well has just made this series <b> one </b> of my favourites of all-time… and considering how many series I’ve read and loved, this speaks volumes.<br /><br />I’m both “very glad” and “very sad” to learn that there is only one more book to finish off this series. This was originally planned as a trilogy but the author has since decided that there needed to be one more book to finish the story and to my personal delight Alex will be sharing the POV for book 4. As I mentioned he’s got a story that needs to be told so this was fantastic news for me. I’m only sad that it will end there. I will miss these characters very much. <br /><br />Bravo Jessica Sorensen! I ADORED IT!!!<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="4936824581014219102" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer1058698974105126577">Oral Assessment - Wide Reading<br/><br/>1.I decided to read this book because it a series and I started with The Fallen Star and got hooked into it, and when I finished the second book in two days I couldn’t wait to start the next book in the series.<br/><br/>2.I found the main character (Gemmas) dad interesting, as the book was about a new mission for Gemma to travel through a crystal ball and stop her dad from changing the vison that he was trapped for changing.   <span id="freeText1058698974105126577" style="display:none">Oral Assessment - Wide Reading<br /><br />1.I decided to read this book because it a series and I started with The Fallen Star and got hooked into it, and when I finished the second book in two days I couldn’t wait to start the next book in the series.<br /><br />2.I found the main character (Gemmas) dad interesting, as the book was about a new mission for Gemma to travel through a crystal ball and stop her dad from changing the vison that he was trapped for changing. Gemmas dad, Julian is an almighty powerful foreseer who had been trapped in his own mind for changing a vison, which is an incredibly bad thing to do amongst the foreseers<br /><br />3.“I kept having these dreams, or maybe they were more like nightmares.” I like this quote because throughout the series, Gemmas character develops further and further. Gemma is faced with many consequences and after she realises who she really is from the first book in the series. She pictures terrifying and bad things all the time. She always doubts herself when she is faced with these challenges, and she cant forget about the horrible things she has faced.<br /><br />4.Gemmas shown as a scared, confused girl but as you keep reading this book she starts to emerge as a strong leader, even though she is still afraid of the challenges and consequences and shows her fear. However with every new surprise she gains strength and bit more personality. This makes you think that even if you are faced with a lot of challenges in your life, you just need face them and let others know that you can get over challenging obstacles and once you get over them you would become and feel like a much stronger person than who you really are.<br /></span>

  <span id="freeText5173525758818902225" style="display:none">This book was so, so good. It answered alot of questions that I had. I wasnt ready for it to end though. I didnt want it to end the way that it did. I WANTED MORE!!!I am so happy there is one more book to this series. The storyline is still evolving. So thats a plus! Overcoming so many hurdles and obstacles. Tackling so many new adventures. Nicholas however is very strange to me, like he doesnt quite fit in with the gang. So I dont know how they will have him end up. Gemma, Alex, Laylen and Aislin I am curious how they will be by the end of the story. I do want to know more about Aislin and Laylen. They havent told too much of their background. I love the characters Gemma and Alex. They are just so strong, especially Gemma she has come along way with not being able to feel. With who she really is. I cant wait to start the next book to see how it will all end.<br />Very Enjoyable, Great Storyline, Great paranormal young adult story. My first series by Jessica Sorenson and it has been so enjoyable!!!!</span>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('qy9sIpkEAYUeK7KdZmi1e+Yhg77sQTz2GPfAPMkKdvYpHhEaWJ7j9R3Uhl399mCjHPbi8fIHsQJMSJg9EkkLMg==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('upVqz2icg4OEVz80F90sAbWD212ZlI8TMNz0mLDW0jM4pBf3qQZh84eoC/SMQ/nZT1S6EofSAudkY6yZa5Wv9w==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>
